<div class="post-body-inner">
<div class="post-message-container" data-role="message-container">
<div class="publisher-anchor-color" data-role="message-content">
<div class="post-message " data-role="message" dir="auto">
<p>Obama affirms ‘one-China’ policy<br>By - The Washington Times - Tuesday, November 17, 2009<br>SHANGHAI (AP) — President Barack Obama says he sees no need to change Washington’s “one-China” policy, which acknowledges China’s position that Taiwan is part of its territory.<br>Taiwan and China split amid civil war in 1949. Beijing threatens to attack if Taiwan moves to formalize its de facto independence.</p>
</div>

<p>I think I said, "I didn't say I was good". For those who like to pick on me by criticizing my writing, I normally would return the favor. Now it is my turn. You wrote, "… trying to correct others by posting a wrong sentence grammatically." Your writing sucks. Wouldn't it be easier for you to just write, "… by posting a grammatically incorrect sentence"? LOL <br>.<br>ROFL...</p>
